is <em>&ldquo;Attack Celebrity&rdquo;</em> (or <em>&ldquo;Attack on Celebrity&rdquo;)</em>, where the production team from the <a Titan</span></strong></em></a> anime series super imposes titan versions of Japanese celebrities into cuts from the anime series and change the blades into Snickers bars.</p> <p style="text-align: a prize pack.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>For the second part of the campaign will start up after the first part has finished. This section <strong>wants people to buy</strong> either the <em>Snickers Peanut Single</em> or <em>Snickers Cacao Strong</em> bars and <strong>tweeting an image of the bar</strong> to the campaigns twitter account. Check out details of the graceful special item after the jump!</p> <p>Following the well-received Rem released in January 2019 and the Ram to be shipped in this December (both from <em>Re:ZERO -Starting Life in Another World-</em>), Tokyo-based Japanese entertainment company Furyu's official EC store F:NEX has strated accepting pre-orders for <span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="https://fnex.jp/products/detail.php?product_id=49" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">its new 1/7 scale figure of Asuna</span></a></span>, one of the main heroines in Reki Kawahara's popular light novel series <em>Sword Art Online</em>, wearing a shiromuku (pure-white) dress.</p> <p>&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> <p>As explained before, a bride wears a white kimono called "shiromuku" and a special silk floss headdress in Japanese traditional Shinto wedding ceremony. And this costume has never been seen in the original <em>Sword Art Online</em> novel and anime story.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Pre-orders for the build-to-order limited 17,400 yen (before tax/about 160 US dollars) item will be accepted until 23:59 on January 7, 2020 (JST), and its scheduled shipping date is March 2020.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <center> <p><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/7288b65561ddea63725c90e3604e02df1569912099_full.jpg" alt="" width="640" height="854" /></p> <p><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/499196e19e5d5629d3c03982e11ef5f41569912112_full.jpg" alt="" width="640" height="854" /></p> <p><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/b24a2d410f19b9533ce5584732149af31569912125_full.jpg" alt="" width="640" height="854" /></p> <p><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/5130d0763da68a5ef06f3eddbe1232c21569912152_full.jpg" alt="" width="640" height="480" /></p> <p><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/f71d16a9e58e029c1806663dc7c5d4161569912167_full.jpg" alt="" width="640" height="854" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The set includes a gold‐leafed folding screen featuring Ainclad's scenery:&nbsp;</p> <p><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/79380ce5e3cff2b182e98d59b70441eb1569912280_full.jpg" alt="" width="640" height="800" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <blockquote class="twitter-tweet"> <p lang="ja" dir="ltr">愛して&hellip; Sump,&nbsp; AKB48, SKE48, and other Japanese idol groups.&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Senda is cast as the anime's main heroine Sally Land, and it is her anime voice acting debut role. She is also an active university student now. She says, <span style="color: #000080;">"I have just debuted as a voice actor, and I will also make my singer debut! I have had nothing but surprises, and it hasn't hit me yet. I really appreciate for this wonderful opportunity! I don't have any experience in singing, but I did my best to sing with all of my heart, so I would be happy if you could listen to it! I hope I can continue to deliver enjoyable and heartfelt songs to you. Thanks!"</span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <center> <blockquote class="twitter-tweet"> <p lang="ja" dir="ltr">声優の千田葉月「ゾイドワイルド ZERO」エンディング曲で歌手デビュー（コメントあり）<a href="https://t.co/R0XQvI6zCc">https://t.co/R0XQvI6zCc</a> <a href="https://t.co/OHvJmzNVRN">pic.twitter.com/OHvJmzNVRN</a></p> &mdash; 音楽ナタリー (@natalie_mu) <a href="https://twitter.com/natalie_mu/status/1178897362053300225?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">October 1, 2019</a></blockquote> </center> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><a href="https://anime-zoidswild-zero.jp/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;"><em><strong>Zoids Wild ZERO</strong></em></span></a>, the second season of the TV anime <a href="https://anime-zoidswild.jp/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;"><em><strong>Zoids Wild</strong></em></span></a>&nbsp;series based on Takara Tommy's sci-fi mechanical animal franchise, is set to premiere on TV Tokyo and its five affiliates in Japan in <strong>October 4, 2019</strong>.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong>Takao Kato</strong>, who directed the first TV anime&nbsp;<em><strong>Zoids</strong></em> (1999-2000) and its sequel&nbsp;<em><strong>Zoids: New Century Slash Zero</strong></em> (2001), returns to the series as director after 18 years, alongside series composition writer <strong>Kennichi Araki</strong> and character designer <strong>Tadashi Sakazaki</strong>. Read special messages from Nanoha VA Yukari Tamura and Fate VA Nana Mizuki after the jump!</p> <p><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/0b9efeb247339e4927b19ebc1cb2e2431569902374_full.jpg" alt="" width="640" height="433" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>To commemorate its 15th anniversary, an official portal site for the <em><strong>Magical Girl Lyrical Nanoha</strong></em> franchise is <a href="https://nanoha.com/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">opened</span></a>&nbsp;with a newly-drawn memorial illustration today on October 1, 2019. Its 13-episode first TV anime series started airing in Japan just 15 years ago from today, October 1, 2004. Read special messages from the franchise's two man voice actresses below.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>Yukari Tamura (Nanoha Takamachi):</strong></span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><span style="color: #000080;"><em>"Congratulations on Lyrical Nanoha's 15th anniversary. I feel nostalgic about the day when we had a press conference for the first Nanoha at King Records' studio. I remember I was excited with so much anticipation at the time. I never thought it would become a series that has continued even until now, 2019. I have experienced many things through the franchise, and have had a lot of fun at each time. 15 years has passed, it still makes me very excited. I am very thankful to be involved in such a wonderful franchise. If there is still something I can do, I would be happy to offer my little help. Happy 15th anniversary!"</em></span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>Nana Mizuki (Fate Testarossa):</strong></span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><span style="color: #000080;"><em>"It has been 15 years since the day when producer Mishima-san, Yukari-san, and I made the presentation at King Records' multi-purpose room by arranging long desks and pipe chairs. After reading Tsuzuki-san's scenario, I was strongly inspired by the character's pure soul and its thrilling story, felt like 'This is the series that I definitely want to deliver to many people!!' Then the entire production team worked so hard. That feeling spread out little by little as the episodes and the series continued. I feel once again that I can't be happier than being beside with Nanoha for such a long time along with all of you. In order to express my gratitude to Nanoha that gave so many 'beginnings' and to those who dedicated all of their love to Nanoha, I will do my best with my biggest love at the 'Lyrical Live' in January next year!! Thank you so much for 15 years!! And thank you for your continued support!!"</em></span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <center> <blockquote class="twitter-tweet"> <p lang="ja" dir="ltr">????NANOHA 15th Anniversary????<br /><br />2004年10月1日にTVアニメ第1期が放送開始した「魔法少女リリカルなのは」シリーズが、本日15周年を迎えました！<br /><br />いつも応援有難うございます！<br />これからも、なのは達を宜しくお願いします！<br /><br />シリーズポータルサイトOPEN‼️<br />▶︎<a href="https://t.co/3UmYJvCaWW">https://t.co/3UmYJvCaWW</a><a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/nanoha15th?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">#nanoha15th</a> <a href="https://t.co/QV1GGmyNxt">pic.twitter.com/QV1GGmyNxt</a></p> &mdash; Well, there is, and in the latest issue of Kodansha's&nbsp;<em>Weekly Young Magazine</em>, Belldandy interviews for a position with the infamous Teiai Group in a comic cross-over with&nbsp;<span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="/mr-tonegawa-middle-management-blues?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><span style="color: #ff9900;"><strong><em>Mr. TONEGAWA Middle Management Blues</em></strong></span></a></span>!</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Oh My Job Hunting Goddess! manga visual" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/5aad5cc09e7dba9dcb3a773f208635081569866536_full.jpg" alt="A page from the cross-over between Oh My Job Hunting Goddess! and Mr. TONEGAWA Middle Management Blues, published in issue 44 of Kodansha's Weekly Young Magazine." width="640" height="909" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong><em>Oh My Job Hunting Goddess!</em></strong>&nbsp;is written by U-hei Aoki and features artwork by Kimuchi Yoshizuki with assistance by&nbsp;Kōsuke Fujishima, the author of the original&nbsp;<strong><em>Oh My Goddess!</em></strong>&nbsp;manga. The unlikely cross-over takes place in the 44th issue of the 2019 print run of&nbsp;<em>Weekly Young Magazine</em>, which was published in Japan on September 30, 2019.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The&nbsp;<span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="/mr-tonegawa-middle-management-blues?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><span style="color: #ff9900;"><strong><em>Mr. TONEGAWA Middle Management Blues</em></strong></span></a></span>&nbsp;manga, which is written by Tensei Hagiwara and illustrated by Tomohiro Hashimoto and Tomoko Miyoshi, is also published by Kodansha, although it now runs in&nbsp;<em>Comic Days</em>&nbsp;rather than&nbsp;<em>Young Magazine</em>.&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Sources:</p> <p><span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="http://jin115.com/archives/52271140.html" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">My Game News Flash</span></a></span></p> <p>Official <em>Weekly Young Magazine</em> Twitter feed (<span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="https://twitter.com/magazine_young" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">@magazine_young</span></a></span>)</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><a href="https://got.cr/PremiumTrial-NewsBanner6"><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Crunchyroll Try Premium For Free Banner" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/f41d6b240e1f788e27a3ff18df8093531569865296_full.png" alt="Hime poses for a Crunchyroll ad banner." width="640" height="43" /></a></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>---</p> <p>Paul Chapman is the host of&nbsp;<a href="http://gmepodcast.com/" target="_blank">The Greatest Movie EVER! Anime Fun Time.</p> Mon, 30 Sep 2019 23:04:05 GMT http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/crunchyroll/animenews/~3/F6wJQcOue54/belldandy-tries-out-for-a-black-company-in-bizarre-manga-cross-over https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/09/30-1/belldandy-tries-out-for-a-black-company-in-bizarre-manga-cross-over https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/09/30-1/belldandy-tries-out-for-a-black-company-in-bizarre-manga-cross-over Studio Ghibli Producer Discusses Nausicaa of the Valley of the Wind Kabuki Stage Play news+feed@crunchyroll.com “Let’s do it”, director Hayao Miyazaki said when presented with the idea<br/><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/bcd3cd53373a094dbe6011fd953ced911569851895_thumb.jpg" /><br/><br/><p>The <em>Nausica&auml; of the Valley of the Wind</em> anime film is one of the many greats from Hayao Miyazaki. Nearly, 40 years on, the film&nbsp;is being adapted into a kabuki play. In a press conference, Toshio Suzuki, a producer at Studio Ghibli, discussed the studio&rsquo;s involvement with the kabuki play and how it came about. Hit the jump to find out more!</p> <p><img title="Nausicaa of the Valley of the Wind kabuki" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/95682b34148084a15176d260b97b40ae1569851696_full.jpg" alt="Nausicaa of the Valley of the Wind kabuki" width="640" height="346" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The <em><strong>Nausica&auml; of the Valley of the Wind</strong></em> anime film is one of the many greats from Hayao Miyazaki, who created the original story ias a manga in 1979 to appease Toshio Suzuki, who was a producer at Animage at the time. 40 years on, <em><strong>Nausica&auml; of the Valley of the Wind</strong></em> is being adapted into a kabuki play to run in Tokyo from December 6 to 25.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>In a <a href="https://natalie.mu/comic/news/349622"><span style="color: #ff9900;">press conference</span></a> about the performance, Suzuki, who has been working as a producer at Studio Ghibli since the films production, discussed the studio&rsquo;s involvement with the kabuki play and how it came about.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><img title="Nausicaa of the Valley of the Wind kabuki" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/659765351173283de95c68bbb1b2441b1569851722_full.jpg" alt="Nausicaa of the Valley of the Wind kabuki" width="640" height="427" /></p> <p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p> <p><em>&ldquo;A kabuki play is easier than a film production, because we (Studio Ghibli) are providing the original work, we are in a position to rely (on others to do the works),&rdquo;</em> Suzuki joked at the conference. Suzuki also discussed Hayao Miyazaki&rsquo;s thoughts on the project, who exclaimed <em>&ldquo;let&rsquo;s do it&rdquo;</em> when presented with the idea of Onoe Kikunosuke V adapting <em><strong>Princess Mononoke</strong></em> into kabuki, thinking Miyazaki would reject it. Onoe Kikunosuke V on the other hand, wanted to adapt Nausica&auml; instead.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Miyazaki only had two requests for the kabuki play. The first is to keep the full original Japanese name <em>&ldquo;Kaze no Tani no Naushika&rdquo;</em>, and for Suzuki to handle all the press conferences and interviews about the play.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><img title="Nausicaa of the Valley of the Wind kabuki" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/7af9cf050ad3fa5cd467ac62358666661569851740_full.jpg" alt="Nausicaa of the Valley of the Wind kabuki" width="640" height="427" /></p> <p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p> <p>Onoe Kikunosuke V, who is playing Nausica&auml;, &ndash; men traditionally play female roles in kabuki, this term is called <em>onnagata (female role specialist)</em> &ndash; said that the play is<em> &ldquo;not only for fans of kabuki, but also for fans of Studio Ghibli.&rdquo;</em> According to him, the play <em>&ldquo;borrows some of his music&rdquo;</em> and that there are <em>&ldquo;scenes of Japanese dance.&rdquo;</em></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Kikunosuke explained that he started preparations for the play <em>&ldquo;about five years ago&rdquo;</em> and that he was attracted to the &ldquo;<em>deep themes of war, environmental issues, nuclear issues&rdquo;</em> and many more. He&rsquo;s <em>&ldquo;excited&rdquo;</em> to see how these themes merge together with kabuki.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The <em><strong>Nausica&auml; of the Valley of the Wind</strong></em> kabuki play is planned to run at Shinbashi Enbujo Theatre in Ginza, Tokyo from December 6 to 25. Tickets go on sale on October 19 at 10 AM.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong>Source: <a href="https://natalie.mu/comic/news/349622"><span style="color: #ff9900;">Comic Natalie</span></a></strong></p> <p><strong><span style="color: #ff9900;"><br /></span></strong></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://got.cr/PremiumTrial-NewsBanner4" target="_blank"><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/78f5441d927cf160a93e037b567c2b1f1563764332_full.png" alt="Try Crunchyroll Premium Today!" width="640" height="43" /></a></p> <p><em>----</em>&nbsp;</p> <p><em>Daryl Harding is a Japan Correspondent for Crunchyroll News. </em>is based on the romantic comedy manga series by Taishi Tsutsui, which is currently serialized in <em>Weekly Shonen Jump </em>magazine. The series launched back in February of 2017, and Viz Media publishes it in English.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Volume 1 cover:</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/0eebcba163d00496c8a9e842e9f5ca341569872325_full.jpg" alt="" width="640" height="960" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The manga's 10th volume was listed among the top 20 best-selling comics in Japan by Oricon.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="https://bokuben-anime.com/"><span style="color: #ff9900;">Official website</span></a></span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://got.cr/PremiumTrial-NewsBanner4"><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/78f5441d927cf160a93e037b567c2b1f1560821317_full.png" alt="" width="640" height="43" /></a></p> <p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p> <p class="p1">-------</p> <p class="p1"><em>Joseph Luster is the Games and Web editor at </em><a href="http://www.otakuusamagazine.com/ME2/Default.asp"><em>Otaku USA Magazine</em></a><em>. what will be her first U.S. appearance.<span class="Apple-converted-space">&nbsp;Read on for more.</span></p> <p class="p1"><img <strong>Anime NYC </strong>event just announced a big guest from the world of Japanese voice acting. <strong>Rie Kugimiya</strong> is officially on board to participate as an Official Guest, with the prolific voice actress set to take part in a main stage panel discussion and a rare autograph session with fans in what will be her first U.S. appearance.<span class="Apple-converted-space">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="p2">&nbsp;</p> <p class="p1">Known to some as the "Queen of Tsundere"&mdash;thanks to portraying many cold-hearted characters since her 1992 debut&mdash;Kugimiya has taken home honors like Best Actress and Best Supporting Role in the prestigious Seiyuu Awards.<span class="Apple-converted-space">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="p2">&nbsp;</p> <p class="p1">Some of her most famous roles include:</p> <p class="p2">&nbsp;</p> <p class="p3"><span class="s1"><strong>Alphonse Elric</strong> (<span style="color: #ff9900;"><a Read on for complete details</p> <p style="text-align: center;" dir="ltr"><img title="King's Raid x DreamCatcher" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/f901210b8c7bd1aa1882b4988fc669201569867500_full.jpg" alt="King's Raid x DreamCatcher" width="639" height="351" />&nbsp;</p> <p dir="ltr">VESPA has announced the release of a new collaboration music video with Korean girl group DreamCatcher to celebrate the New Season of King&rsquo;s Raid &ldquo;Soul Weapon&rdquo;. &ldquo;Deja Vu&rdquo; is the first song to be featured by developer Vespa for hit mobile game King&rsquo;s Raid -Soul Weapon-. The music video was released on September 18th and is the start of a&nbsp; long-term collaboration between developer Vespa and DreamCatcher. The <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gpcKU_Zjyh0">music video</a> has garnered over 2.8 million views and climbing.</p> <p style="text-align: center;" dir="ltr">&nbsp;<img title="King's Raid logo" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/8e95709635d4c25e3489a07e34bd9a531569867614_full.jpg" alt="King's Raid logo" width="512" height="418" /></p> <p dir="ltr">Alongside the release of the music video, VESPA has also updated KING&rsquo;S RAID with a new update called &ldquo;Soul Weapon.&rdquo; &ldquo;Soul Weapon&rdquo; is a new update full of Unique Weapons and related items to unleash the full power of your heroes, and includes a variety of content including &ldquo;The King&rsquo;s Sanctum&rdquo; to unleash &ldquo;Soul Weapons&rdquo;, &ldquo;Trial of the God King&rdquo; to gather related materials, and &ldquo;Eclipse&rdquo; to fight endless waves of battles under the Red Moon.&nbsp;</p> <p dir="ltr">&nbsp;</p> <p dir="ltr">The &ldquo;Soul Weapon&rdquo; update will open with the introduction of &ldquo;Immortal King Cain&rdquo; when players clear stage 6-21 in-game. After completing all the storyline for Cain, &ldquo;The King&rsquo;s Sanctum&rdquo; will be unlocked which will lead to other content in the update such as &ldquo;Soul Weapon&rdquo;, &ldquo;Trial of the God King&rdquo;, and &ldquo;Eclipse.&rdquo;</p> <p dir="ltr">&nbsp;</p> <p dir="ltr">The &ldquo;Soul Weapon&rdquo; content will be open to anyone when they acquire Unique Weapons and does not require the Unique Weapons to be fully upgraded in order to gain access. A total of 20 &ldquo;Soul Weapons&rdquo; will be introduced through this update and the heroes receiving their weapons are Jane, Theo, Laudia, Annette, Laias, and more. By using the materials gained from the &ldquo;Trial of the God King,&rdquo; players can fully unleash the potential of their Unique Weapons. &ldquo;Soul Weapons&rdquo; provide a stat boost and additional skill capabilities that match each heroes capabilities.&nbsp;</p> <p dir="ltr"><br />&ldquo;Immortal King Cain&rdquo; will also be introduced as a new NPC hero. Cain is a wizard class hero with outstanding combat and physical damage skills, but also helps in healing allies and increasing their armor points. Cain will be 100% obtainable for anyone who clears the &ldquo;Temple of the God King&rdquo; storyline and will provide a 20% increased attack buff for all allies in the new &ldquo;Eclipse&rdquo; content.</p> <p dir="ltr">&nbsp;</p> <p dir="ltr">VESPA is also planning to provide plenty of bonuses through the 14-day login rewards campaign which includes the Unique Weapon Selector, an entrance ticket to &ldquo;Trial of the God King&rdquo;, and the materials required for the new update to help anyone who plays KING&rsquo;S RAID a chance to build their &ldquo;Soul Weapons.&rdquo;</p> <p dir="ltr">&nbsp;</p> <p dir="ltr">For more detailed information about &ldquo;Soul Weapons,&rdquo; you can visit KING&rsquo;S RAID&rsquo;s Facebook page at (<a href="https://www.facebook.com/Kingsraid.EN/">https://www.facebook.com/Kingsraid.EN/</a>) or the main page (<a href="https://www.kingsraid.com/?lang=en/">https://www.kingsraid.com/?lang=en/</a>).&nbsp;</p> <div><span><br /></span></div> Mon, 30 Sep 2019 18:45:00 GMT http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/crunchyroll/animenews/~3/5ZkeGKUn5Tk/sponsored-post-kings-raid-x-dreamcatcher-collaboration-music-video-deja-vu-released-new-update-soul-weapon-announced https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/09/30/sponsored-post-kings-raid-x-dreamcatcher-collaboration-music-video-deja-vu-released-new-update-soul-weapon-announced https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/09/30/sponsored-post-kings-raid-x-dreamcatcher-collaboration-music-video-deja-vu-released-new-update-soul-weapon-announced Crunchyroll Heads East to New York Comic Con! news+feed@crunchyroll.com See what's in store for this year's event! <br/><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/d117bb9d0da8682598de2c74ac60e92b1569851786_thumb.jpg" /><br/><br/><p class="p1"><span class="s1">It&rsquo;s been a blast West Coast, but now&nbsp;it&rsquo;s time for Crunchyroll to head back East. There's no time to catch up on everything in time, but what exactly should you prioritize? Today on Why It Works, let's break down the various appeals of the coming season's acclaimed sequels!</p> <p dir="ltr"><span><a href="https://twitter.com/B0bduh" target="_blank"><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/4c07afa4af0d7ba70dbd674a0763e3911549720139_full.png" alt="nickcreamer" /></a></span></p> <p dir="ltr"><br />Hey folks, and welcome back to Why It Works. The summer season&rsquo;s basically over at this point, and all eyes are pointed towards the upcoming fall premieres. It&rsquo;s often hard to discern what new shows might emerge as seasonal favorites, but in this upcoming fall season&rsquo;s case, we&rsquo;ve got such a wide array of long-awaited sequels that I imagine most of you already have a few picks in mind. If you&rsquo;re wondering what all Crunchyroll will be streaming this fall, we&rsquo;ve <span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong><a href="/anime-news/2019/09/18-1/crunchyroll-announces-fall-2019-anime-lineup?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=carousel&amp;utm_campaign=hime-in-lights&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_carousel_hime-in-lights?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;">already got you covered</span></a></strong></span> with a list of all the currently-announced productions; but of course, a picture and a synopsis can only tell you so much.</p> <p dir="ltr">&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;" dir="ltr"><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/ee0489bef5f0c8222d5b78ffd353ee631569682586_full.jpg" alt="myheroacademia" width="640" height="360" /></p> <p><span><span><br /></span></span></p> <p dir="ltr"><span>For a more personal approach, today I&rsquo;ve got, well, me, I guess. While the list of totally new premieres has yet to be filled out, we&rsquo;ve already got a wide array of sequels on the approach, each of them with their own unique merits. I can&rsquo;t in good conscious ask you to catch up with literally everything, but I </span><span>can</span><span> hopefully provide some context as to which of these continuing series might best suit your anime needs. So as briefly as possible, let&rsquo;s run down the unique appeals of next season&rsquo;s continuing favorites!</span></p> <p><span><span><br /></span></span></p> <p dir="ltr"><span>First off, </span><em><span style="color: #ff6600;"><a href="/my-hero-academia?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>My Hero Academia</strong></span></a></span></em><span> is probably the highest-profile returning show, and for good reason<span>&mdash;</span>it&rsquo;s an altogether excellent shonen adventure, produced by an incredibly strong team at Studio BONES. </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em>My Hero Academia</em></span><span> is likely the best all-around recommendation, featuring an endearing cast, a unique and convincing world, beautifully animated fight scenes, and plenty of creative twists and turns. In the same way that <em><span style="color: #ff6600;"><a href="/naruto?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>Naruto</strong></span></a></span></em> is essentially &ldquo;ninja world shonen&rdquo; and <em><span style="color: #ff6600;"><a href="/one-piece?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>One Piece</strong></span></a></span></em> is &ldquo;pirate world shonen,&rdquo; <em><span style="color: #ff6600;">My Hero Academia</span></em> is &ldquo;superhero world shonen&rdquo;, and it really does live up to its famous predecessors.</span></p> <p dir="ltr"><span><br /></span></p> <p style="text-align: center;" dir="ltr"><span><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/c22b4447c2e60609c85dfe1a630acc911569683103_full.jpg" alt="chihayafuru" width="640" height="360" /></span></p> <p><span><span><br /></span></span></p> <p dir="ltr"><span>Beyond </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em>My Hero Academia</em></span><span>, recommendations get a bit more specific. Personally, my own most highly-anticipated show is </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em><a href="/chihayafuru?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>Chihayafuru</strong></span></a></em></span><span>, which will be commencing its third season after six long years off the air. I <span style="color: #ff6600;"><a href="/anime-feature/2019/09/16/its-time-to-get-caught-up-for-next-seasons-chihayafuru?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>recently wrote</strong></span></a></span> a full-length pitch for <em><span style="color: #ff9900;">C<span style="color: #ff6600;">hihayafuru</span></span></em> specifically, but in short, I consider it one of the very best sports anime of all time, and a true champion when it comes to thrilling tournament arcs and tactics-oriented battles. If you enjoy the clever mental battles of a show like </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em><a href="/hunter-x-hunter?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>Hunter x Hunter</strong></span></a></em></span><span>, you might be surprised by how much you enjoy </span><span>Chihayafuru</span><span>.</span></p> <p><span><span><br /></span></span></p> <p dir="ltr"><span>That said, if you prefer wild stylistic flourishes and boundless, over-the-top energy, this coming season&rsquo;s top pick could easily be </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em><a href="/food-wars-shokugeki-no-soma?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>Food Wars!</strong></span></a></em></span><span>&nbsp;</span><span>It's a show that attacks the process of food preparation with the creativity and bombast of something like </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><a href="/jojos-bizarre-adventure?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>JoJo&rsquo;s Bizarre Adventure</strong></span></a></span><span>, as competitive cooks send each other into orgasmic reveries of culinary chaos. Meanwhile, those looking for something grounded in real-world variables and full of clever ideas, </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em><a href="/dr-stone?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>Dr. STONE</strong></span></a></em></span><span>&nbsp;offers a shonen adventure like few others. If </span><span>My Hero Academia</span><span> is &ldquo;superhero world,&rdquo; then </span><em><span style="color: #ff6600;">Dr. STONE&nbsp;</span></em><span>might well be &ldquo;mad scientist world&rdquo;<span>&mdash;</span>a show set on a post-apocalyptic earth, where humanity&rsquo;s survivors must rebuild human civilization one key invention at a time. </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em>Dr. STONE</em></span><span>&rsquo;s unique conceit more than makes up for its relatively conservative adaptation, simultaneously appealing as an energetic adventure narrative and an informative &ldquo;how things work&rdquo;-style program.</span></p> <p dir="ltr"><span><br /></span></p> <p style="text-align: center;" dir="ltr"><span><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/9b82e3c490781b49e04e6fe41f601c0d1569684292_full.jpg" alt="blackclover" width="640" height="360" /></span></p> <p><span><span><br /></span></span></p> <p dir="ltr"><span>Moving right along, we have two more relatively straightforward shonen adventures: the relatively new </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong><em><a href="/radiant?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;">RADIANT</span></a></em></strong></span><span>, and the continuing&nbsp;</span><span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em><a href="/black-clover?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>Black Clover</strong></span></a></em></span>.</span><span> Both of these series follow a more traditional &ldquo;shonen adventure in a fantasy-magic world&rdquo; path, though they each have their own quirks. </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em>RADIANT</em></span><span> is actually based on a french comic, and boasts lots of uniquely appealing world design elements, while </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em>Black Clover</em></span><span> has been blessed by some of the most talented young animators in the industry, making its recent action highlights into something <a href="https://www.sakugabooru.com/post/show/86844" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;"><strong><span style="color: #ff6600;">truly spectacular</span></strong></span></a>. If you want to see some of the best new animators making their first major marks on the industry, you should definitely keep an eye on the action-packed </span><span>Clover</span><span>.</span></p> <p><span><span><br /></span></span></p> <p dir="ltr"><span>And finally, I&rsquo;d be profoundly negligent in my responsibilities if I didn&rsquo;t highlight the one true sequel of the fall season: </span><span style="color: #ff9900;"><strong><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em>Bananya</em></span> </strong><span style="color: #000000;">Season 2</span></span><span>. As we learned in </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><a href="/bananya?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong>Bananya</strong></span></a></span><span>&rsquo;s triumphant first season, </span><span style="color: #ff6600;"><em>Bananya</em></span><span> is a show about a cat who is also a banana. That&rsquo;s it. That&rsquo;s the whole show.</span></p> <p><span id="docs-internal-guid-44ba4195-7fff-b450-9b21-1f5a28f0c4c1"><br /><span>I hope at least one of these formidable franchises sparked your interest, and if not, there are still plenty of other new properties approaching this fall. <em><strong>Either way, </strong></em></span><em><strong>please let me know what you&rsquo;re all most looking forward to in the comments!</strong></em></span></p> <p dir="ltr"><span><a href="https://got.cr/PremiumTrial-NewsBanner4" target="_blank"><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/02e67bba17e5d0b163e23120db4a2d911555895980_full.png" alt="Try Crunchyroll Premium for Free!" /></a></span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>-----</p> <p><em>Nick Creamer has been writing about cartoons for too many years now, and is always ready to cry about Madoka. In this setting, various "Divers" play the game and pilot their mecha, including Hiroto Kuga, a Builder / Diver who is searching for another player with whom he has lost contact.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="GUNDAM BUILD DIVERS Re:RISE key visual" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/2ee5c1e18fee1a531ddc54c3b090e9e01566739500_full.jpg" alt="A key visual for GUNDAM BUILD DIVERS Re:RISE featuring the main characters and their dueling Gunpla mecha in the GBA virtual environment." width="640" height="897" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong><em>GUNDAM BUILD DIVERS Re:RISE</em></strong>&nbsp;is directed by Shinya Watada and features animation production by Sunrise Beyond. The series will simulcast on Youtube on Thursdays during the 20:00 time slot (8:00pm JST) beginning on October 10, 2019, and it will also broadcast on BS11 on Saturdays during the 19L00 time slot (7:00pm JST) beginning on October 12, 2019.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Source: <a href="https://natalie.mu/comic/news/349613" target="_blank">Comic Natalie</a></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><a href="https://got.cr/PremiumTrial-NewsBanner3"><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Crunchyroll Watch Anime Ad Free Banner" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/3a6c87cdb22e3852b4c3a37cfe5cea441569850884_full.png" alt="Hime poses for a Crunchyroll ad banner." width="640" height="43" /></a></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>---</p> <p>Paul Chapman is the host of&nbsp;<a href="http://gmepodcast.com/" target="_blank">The Greatest Movie EVER! TV Anime news+feed@crunchyroll.com Adaptation based on isekai fantasy light novel series hits Japanese TV and Crunchyroll in Fall of 2019<br/><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/b74bc18d58e173bfc481766f8dfa7b971569849923_thumb.png" /><br/><br/><p>Three more cast members have been revealed for <em>Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?!</em>, an upcoming TV anime based on the isekai fantasy light novel series written by FUNA and illustrated by Itsuki Akata about a young lady who finds her power level skewed a little too high after being reincarnated in a world of magic and adventure. Hit the jump to learn more.</p> <p><img title="Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?! hero image" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/4cf8da1feac2dd4600041a9f904c0b171569849500_full.jpg" alt="Monika, Marcela, and Aureana are a group of young ladies who befriend the protagonist in the Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?! TV Anime." width="600" height="338" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Three more cast members have been revealed for&nbsp;<strong><em>Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?!</em></strong>, an upcoming TV anime based on the isekai fantasy light novel series written by FUNA and illustrated by Itsuki Akata about a young lady who finds her power level skewed a little too high after being reincarnated in a world of magic and adventure.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Wonder Three character visual" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/45aa9d0ef268b7396fab30a38e8a48651569849720_full.jpg" alt="A character visual of the Wonder Three - Marcela, Monika, and Aureana - and their respective voice actresses - Maki Kawase, Kiyono Yasuno, and Hisako Tojo." width="640" height="747" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The new cast members include (above, from left to right):</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <ul> <li>Maki Kawase as <strong>Marcela</strong>.</li> <li>Kiyono Yasuno as <strong>Monika</strong>.</li> <li>And Hisako Tojo as <strong>Aureana</strong>.</li> </ul> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Marcela, Monika, and Aureana are friends of Mile, the main character of&nbsp;<strong><em>Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?!</em></strong>. They attend the same school as Mile, and later they form a Hunter Party known as the "Wonder Three".</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><iframe style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Qz0FJ33W41U" frameborder="0" width="640" height="360"></iframe></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The original&nbsp;<strong><em>Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?!</em></strong>&nbsp;novels are published in Japan by Earth Star Entertainment, and an English language version of the series is also available from Seven Seas Entertainment, who describe the story as follows:</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><em>When she turns ten years old, Adele von Ascham is hit with a horrible headache&ndash;and memories of her previous life as an eighteen-year-old Japanese girl named Kurihara Misato. That life changed abruptly, however, when Misato died trying to aid a little girl and met god. During that meeting, she made an odd request and asked for average abilities in her next life. But few things&ndash;especially wishes&ndash;ever go quite as planned.</em></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?! key visual" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/a7179bb8a8b388a628a57778fe0cb8591566965660_full.jpg" alt="A key visual for the Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?! TV anime, featuring the main character, Mile, and her three adventuring companions: Reina, Mavis, and Pauline." width="564" height="800" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The&nbsp;<strong><em>Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?!</em></strong>&nbsp;TV anime is directed by Masahiko Ohta and features animation production by&nbsp;project No.9. The series will broadcast in Japan on Tokyo AT-X, Tokyo MX, and BS11 beginning on October 07, 2019, with additional broadcasts to follow later on TV Aichi and Asahi Broadcasting Corporation.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong><em>Didn't I Say to Make My Abilities Average in the Next Life?!&nbsp;</em></strong>will also stream on Crunchyroll as part of the Fall 2019 anime simulcast lineup in territories worldwide (except Asia).</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Source: <span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="https://natalie.mu/comic/news/349649" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">Comic Natalie</span></a></span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><a href="https://natalie.mu/comic/news/349649" target="_blank"><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Watch Black Clover on Crunchyroll Banner" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/39b49bb8e240dc3739e26288ac9562e31569849195_full.png" alt="Asta from Black Clover poses with his massive sword for a Crunchyroll ad banner." width="640" height="43" /></a></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>---</p> <p>Paul Chapman is the host of&nbsp;<a href="http://gmepodcast.com/" target="_blank">The Greatest Movie EVER! http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/crunchyroll/animenews/~3/wi_Krc4Mipo/japanese-fans-pick-their-most-anticipated-tv-anime-in-fall-2019 https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/09/30/japanese-fans-pick-their-most-anticipated-tv-anime-in-fall-2019 https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/09/30/japanese-fans-pick-their-most-anticipated-tv-anime-in-fall-2019 Suicide Death Game Begins in Signal 100 Live-Action Film Teaser Trailer news+feed@crunchyroll.com The tagline: "88 minutes of Insanity and Despair."<br/><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/1b36facc8d76c2fddadc6384b2944f6d1569820532_thumb.jpg" /><br/><br/><p>The official website for the forthcoming live-action film adaptation of Arata Miyatsuki (story) and Shigure Kondo (art)'s suspense manga <em><strong>Signal 100</strong></em> has posted a 30-second teaser trailer introducing the beginning of its death game. (Warning: this film is rated "R15+" in Japan)</p> <p>The official website for <a href="http://www.signal100.jp/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">the forthcoming live-action film adaptation</span></a> of Arata Miyatsuki (story) and Shigure Kondo (art)'s suspense manga <em><strong>Signal 100</strong></em> has posted a 30-second teaser trailer introducing the beginning of its death game.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>And in addition to the previously announced 20-year-old <strong>Kanna Hashimoto</strong> (Kagura in <em>Gintama</em>, Kaguya Shinomiya in <em>Kaguya-sama: Love Is War</em>) as the protagonist Rena Kashimura, <strong>Yuta Koseki</strong> (Eiji Kukumaru in <em>The Prince of Tennis Musical</em>),<strong> Toshiki Seto</strong> (Hiiro Kagami/Kamen Rider Brave in <em>Kamen Rider Ex-Aid</em>), and <strong>Shido Nakamura</strong> (Anno Tanaka in <em>Fearless</em>), are also confirmed to be in the cast.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The film is directed by <strong>Lisa Takeba</strong> (<em>Haruko's Paranormal Laboratory</em>) on a screenplay by <strong>Yusuke Watanabe</strong> (<em>Attack on Titan</em> live-action films), and will open in Japan on January 24, 2020, distributed by Toei.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong>(Warning: this film itself is rated "R15+" in Japan, which means "for persons aged 15 and above only. Hit the jump for more details.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>It is officially confirmed today that 46-year-old actress <strong>Rie Miyazawa</strong> makes a special guest voice appearance as Hitomi Nakayama in <a href="http://7dayswar.jp/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">the forthcoming anime film adaptation</span></a> of Osamu Souda's juvenile novel <strong><em>Bokura no Nanokakan Sensou / Seven Days War</em></strong>.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Miyazawa, 15 years old at the time, played her first leading role Hitomi Nakayama in the novel's first live-action adaptation film in August 1988, and won the Newcomer of the Year award in Japan Academy Prize. Her character in the anime film is introduced as "Hitomi Nakayama in 2020." It means that the anime film is a sequel to the live-action film, set about thirty years after.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>It is a similar approach to Mamoru Hosoda's 2006 anime film <em>The Girl Who Leapt Through Time</em>. It was set twenty years after Nobuhiko Obayashi's 1983 live-action film adaptation of Yasutaka Tsutsui's original <em>The Girl Who Leapt Through Time</em> novel, and the original heroine Kazuko Yoshiyama made a guest appearance.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Miyazawa says, "Although it is a small appearance, I participated the anime film as Hitomi Nakayama. As my debut film 'Seven Days War' has been remained deep in the audience's memories at the time, I hope this anime film, which is given a new timeless breath, will be also able to shake your heart. Its five-day sales is 37,483 units.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Aqours' top-ranking single in their four-year activity was <strong>"Bokura no Hashittekita Michi wa/Next SPARKLING!!,"</strong> the OP/ED theme song CD for the <em>Love Live! Sunshine!! The School Idol Movie Over the Rainbow</em> film. The anime special will be based off the second version of the prototype series that <em>One Piece</em> was based off. Hit the jump to set sail and learn more!</p> <p><img title="One Piece Romance Dawn" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/dba9122346e64068917fd0c91c59e0fa1569742778_full.jpg" alt="One Piece Romance Dawn" width="640" height="348" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>After 20 years on the air, the <a href="/one-piece?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><em><strong><span style="color: #ff9900;">One Piece</span></strong></em></a> anime series is still going strong. With over 900 episodes, and a new film just released in Japan, the <a href="/one-piece?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><span style="color: #ff9900;"><em><strong>One Piece</strong></em></span></a> ship won&rsquo;t be making port anytime soon. To celebrate the 20th anniversary of the first episode airing on Japanese TV screens, Toei Animation will be adapting Version 2 of &lsquo;<strong><em>Romance Dawn.&rsquo;</em></strong> A trailer was <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jfI1MQ9rhEo"><span style="color: #ff9900;">streamed</span></a> on the <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCdAHaWcKdpbT5XkN2Er6BUQ"><span style="color: #ff9900;">official One Piece YouTube channel</span></a> on September 29.</p> <p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/jfI1MQ9rhEo" frameborder="0" width="640" height="360"></iframe></p> <p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p> <p><em><strong>Romance Dawn</strong></em> was a prototype of One Piece that was published in Weekly Shonen Jump in 1996. There were two versions of <em><strong>Romance Dawn</strong></em> created before the full serialisation of One Piece. Version 1 of <em><strong>Romance Dawn</strong></em> was adapted into a special in 2008 at the 40th JUMP Super Anime Tour. The 'Romance Dawn' name was used for the first chapter of the <a href="/one-piece?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><em><strong><span style="color: #ff9900;">One Piece</span></strong></em></a> manga as a reference to the prototype versions.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The adaption of Version 2 of <em><strong>Romance Dawn</strong></em>, unlike Version 1, is said to follow the prototype manga more closely without the rest of the Straw Hat crew.&nbsp;The one-shot prototype manga was released in the Wanted! Eiichiro Oda Short Story compilation book in 1998.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Currently, the <a href="/one-piece?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><em><strong><span style="color: #ff9900;">One Piece</span></strong></em></a> anime is in the popular Wano Kuni Arc, which you can watch <a href="/one-piece?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><span style="color: #ff9900;">right here</span></a> on Crunchyroll!</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong>Source: <span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="https://youtu.be/jfI1MQ9rhEo"><span style="color: #ff9900;">Official One Piece YouTube Channel</span></a></span></strong></p> <p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://got.cr/PremiumTrial-NewsBanner4" target="_blank"><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/78f5441d927cf160a93e037b567c2b1f1563764332_full.png" alt="Try Crunchyroll Premium Today!" width="640" height="43" /></a>&nbsp;</p> <p><em>----</em>&nbsp;</p> <p><em>Daryl Harding is a Japan Correspondent for Crunchyroll News. The song will be composed by Yusuke Kato with lyrics by Shin Furuya. The duo also composed the <a href="/zombie-land-saga?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong><em>ZOMBIE LAND SAGA</em></strong></span></a>&nbsp;opening theme, "Adabana Necromancy."</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/O9VOud8y3tg" frameborder="0" width="560" height="315"></iframe></p> <p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: left;">This isn't the first time anime idols have performed a curry-centric song for Nissin. The girls of <a href="/the-idolmster-cinderella-girls?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong><em>iDOLM@STER</em></strong></span></a>&nbsp;unit Positive Passion performed another collab song, "Spice Paradise," in September of last year:</p> <p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/1uRAX4mVc5M" frameborder="0" width="560" height="315"></iframe></p> <p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: left;">Curry Meshi is also apparently preparing to announce even more collaborations in the coming days. How massive? It took 50 employees two days to recreate the Battle of Astarte... using snack food. Check out the video of the process after the jump!</p> <p><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/3e0a435353bb8325ce6fd20ca208d5951569709273_full.png" alt="" width="640" height="360" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Everyone's getting excited for the next stage of <a href="/legend-of-the-galactic-heroes-die-neue-these?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong><em>Legend of the Galactic Heroes: Die Neue These</em></strong></span></a>. Among them are the people behind the Japanese snack Umaibo, who used the popular treat to recreate an epic battle from the show.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The Battle of Astarte appears in both the OVA and the latest anime adaptation, as the Free Planets Alliance and the Galactic Empire face each other down with a total of 60,000 warships in play (40,000 to the Alliance, 20,000 to the Empire). Umaibo decided to make this happen again... but this time, they used their special edition&nbsp;<a href="/legend-of-the-galactic-heroes-die-neue-these?utm_source=editorial_cr&amp;utm_medium=news&amp;utm_campaign=article_driven&amp;referrer=editorial_cr_news_article_driven"><span style="color: #ff6600;"><strong><em>Legend of the Galactic Heroes</em></strong></span></a>&nbsp;snacks to make up the troops:</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/3ce8dd700520f4a219c5dafc6baaad0a1569713837_full.png" alt="" width="640" height="668" /></p> <p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: left;">The special wrappers are being released just in time for the new films, and feature mascot Umaemon dressed as heroes from both sides of the war.</p> <p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: left;">How did it turn out? Check out the video featuring both the setup and the layout intercut with scenes from the anime. Hit the jump to learn more.</p> <p><img title="PROMARE hero image" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/161d6a12c01c585dd30e2fecf1a8b86e1569686811_full.jpg" alt="Galo Thymos from the 2019 anime theatrical film, Promare, directed by Hiroyuki Imaishi and animated by Studio TRIGGER." width="639" height="360" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The <span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="https://2019.tiff-jp.net/en/"><span style="color: #ff9900;">32nd Tokyo International Film Festival</span></a></span> is heading to various venues in Minato Ward, Tokyo, Japan in late October and early November of 2019, and this year they've got a special programming track with a killer lineup dedicated to the history of anime and visual effects TV shows entitled "The Evolution of Japanese Animation / VFX". Screenings include:</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="The White Snake enchantress hero image" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire1/382ab86ce3b5fc384399c64e62b2fe081569687165_full.jpg" alt="A promotional still from the 1958 film, The White Snake Enchantress, commonly believed to be the first feature length anime theatrical film." width="639" height="360" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><strong><em>The White Snake Enchantress</em></strong> (1958), directed by Taiji Yabushita, also known as "Panda and the Magic Serpent".</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Aim for the Best, Theatrical Version hero image" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/07e640f33032262e1cf0d97316c0ec991569687289_full.jpg" alt="A promotional image for Aim for the Best, Theatrical Version, a 1979 compilation film based on the Aim for the Ace TV anime." width="639" height="360" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><em><strong>Aim for the Best, Theatrical Version</strong></em> (1979), directed by Osamu Dezaki, also known as "Aim for the Ace".</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="AKIRA key visual" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/8f4ccdadfbd296d2f327e97050a08f651569687446_full.jpg" alt="The movie poster for the landmark 1988 anime theatrical film, AKIRA, featuring Kaneda posing with a laser rifle against the backdrop of a cybernetic Neo Tokyo." width="640" height="846" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><strong><em>AKIRA</em></strong> (1988), directed by Katsuhiro Otomo.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Children of the Sea hero image" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/b3eee76847b987fea6f8e2aecc29c9261569687570_full.jpg" alt="A promotional image from the 2019 anime theatrical film, Children of the Sea." width="639" height="360" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><strong><em>Children of the Sea</em></strong> (2019), directed by Ayumu Watanabe.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Ride Your Wave hero image" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire4/f9da785c96248e29b57c8820a4497ed81569687655_full.jpg" alt="A promotional image from the 2019 anime theatrical film, Ride Your Wave, featuring the two main characters meeting underwater." width="639" height="360" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><strong><em>Ride Your Wave</em></strong> (2019), directed by Masaaki Yuasa.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Weathering With You hero image" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire3/c551007df0109157cd3fa71057f16b851569688516_full.jpg" alt="A promotional image featuring the main characters of the 2019 anime theatrical film, Weathering With You, standing among an unusual atmospheric effect." width="640" height="429" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: center;"><strong><em>Weathering With You</em></strong> (2019), directed by Makoto Shinkai.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; episode of the 1966 Ultra Q tokusatsu TV series, featuring the titular monster attacking Tokyo Tower." width="639" height="360" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>The&nbsp;"The Evolution of Japanese Animation / VFX" also includes 4K restored screenings of four episodes of the 1966 tokusatsu TV series, <strong><em>Ultra Q</em></strong>: "Challenge from the Year 2020", "Garamon Strikes Back", "Tokyo Ice Age", and "Kanegon's Cocoon". While evading the clutches of the empire and facing off against fearsome primal beasts, the duo felt their bond deepening&mdash;their lives changing.</em></div> <div>&nbsp;</div> <div><em>But despite these tribulations, they're still a long way away from their elusive destination.</em></div> <div>&nbsp;</div> <div><em>The boy and girl, accompanied by fellow seekers of adventure, depart once more into the vast blue skies.</em></div> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="GRANBLUE FANTASY: The Animation Season 2 key visual 2" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/d33c04bd97ca99da50fb2890aee6ca251569674243_full.jpg" alt="A new key visual for GRANBLUE FANTASY: The Animation Season 2 featuring the main cast posing against the backdrop of a cloud-filled sky." width="640" height="907" /></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong><em>GRANBLUE FANTASY: The Animation Season 2</em></strong>&nbsp;is directed by Yui Umemoto and features animation production by MAPPA. The series will broadcast on Tokyo MX, Tochigi TV, Gunma Television, and BS11 beginning on October 04, 2019, with additional broadcasts to follow later on Mainichi Broadcasting System and AT-X.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong><em>GRANBLUE FANTASY: The Animation Season 2</em></strong>&nbsp;will also stream on Crunchyroll in&nbsp;<span>North America, Latin America, the United Kingdom, Ireland, Australia</span><span>, and&nbsp;</span><span>New Zealand</span><span>&nbsp;as part of the Fall 2019 anime simulcast lineup beginning on&nbsp;</span><span>October 04, 2019, at 9:30am Pacific.</span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Sources:</p> <p><span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="https://moca-news.net/article/20190928/2019092815420a_/01/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">MoCa</span></a></span></p> <p><span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="https://natalie.mu/comic/news/349389" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">Comic Natalie</span></a></span></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><a href="https://got.cr/BlackClover-NewsBanner"><img style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Watch Black Clover on Crunchyroll Banner" src="https://img1.ak.crunchyroll.com/i/spire2/39b49bb8e240dc3739e26288ac9562e31569674202_full.png" alt="Asta from Black Clover poses with his massive sword for a Crunchyroll ad banner." width="640" height="43" /></a></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>---</p> <p>Paul Chapman is the host of&nbsp;<a href="http://gmepodcast.com/" target="_blank">The Greatest Movie EVER!
